**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/kafka--be816b82`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kafka--be816b82$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/kafka--be816b82` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-kafka-bug-001: Kafka Producer Buffer Pool Reuse Race Condition

## Task

Investigate a bug in the Apache Kafka producer where a race condition in the `BufferPool` memory management causes messages to silently appear on the wrong topic. Trace the execution path from the producer's `send()` method through batch accumulation, buffer allocation, and network transmission to identify how buffer reuse can corrupt in-flight produce requests.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/kafka--be816b82 (mirror of apache/kafka) (Java, ~800K LOC)
- **Category**: Bug Investigation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Entry Point**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java` — `sendProducerData()` and `failBatch()` methods

## Symptom

Users of the Kafka producer with non-zero `linger.ms` observe that messages published to topic A occasionally appear on topic B instead. The corruption is rare but occurs in bursts, typically during broker restarts or network disruptions. The CRC checksum on the records passes because it covers only key/value/headers, not the topic name. The produce request header (containing topic/partition) is serialized separately from the message payload.

The bug is a race condition: when an in-flight `ProducerBatch` expires or its broker disconnects, the batch's pooled `ByteBuffer` is returned to the `BufferPool` and immediately reused by a new batch — while the original batch's request is still being written to the network by the `Sender` thread.

## Requirements

1. Starting from the entry point, trace the execution path to the root cause
2. Identify the specific file(s) and line(s) where the bug originates
3. Explain WHY the bug occurs (not just WHERE) — focus on the buffer lifecycle
4. Propose a fix with specific code changes

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — examined for [reason]
- path/to/file2.ext — examined for [reason]
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Symptom observed in: path/to/symptom.ext
2. Called from: path/to/caller.ext (function name)
3. Bug triggered by: path/to/buggy.ext (function name, line ~N)
...

## Root Cause
- **File**: path/to/root_cause.ext
- **Function**: function_name()
- **Line**: ~N
- **Explanation**: [Why this code is buggy]

## Proposed Fix
```diff
- buggy code
+ fixed code
```

## Analysis
[Detailed trace from symptom to root cause, explaining each step]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- Root cause identification: Did you find the correct file(s) where the bug originates?
- Call chain accuracy: Did you trace the correct path from symptom to root cause?
- Fix quality: Is the proposed fix correct and minimal?

     1→# Kafka Producer Buffer Pool Race Condition - Analysis and Fix
     2→
     3→## Files Examined
     4→
     5→- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java** — Entry point for bug investigation; contains `sendProducerData()` and `failBatch()` methods
     6→- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/ProducerBatch.java** — Batch lifecycle management; contains `records()` and `completeExceptionally()` methods
     7→- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/RecordAccumulator.java** — Buffer pool management; contains `deallocate()` method
     8→- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/BufferPool.java** — Buffer memory pooling (referenced via RecordAccumulator)
     9→
    10→## Dependency Chain
    11→
    12→1. **Symptom observed in**: Produce requests silently corrupt topic/partition information; messages appear on wrong topic
    13→2. **Called from**: `Sender.sendProducerData()` (line 357) — orchestrates batch draining, expiration, and sending
    14→3. **Batch lifecycle**:
    15→   - Line 395: Batches drained from accumulator
    16→   - Line 396: Batches added to `inFlightBatches` tracking map
    17→   - Line 406-408: Expired batches detected from `inFlightBatches`
    18→   - Line 418: `failBatch()` called on expired batches
    19→   - Line 442: `sendProduceRequests()` sends non-expired batches to network client
    20→4. **Buffer deallocation path**:
    21→   - Line 835: `failBatch()` calls `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` (line 173)
    22→   - Line 173: Calls `accumulator.deallocate(batch)`
    23→   - RecordAccumulator line 1032: Buffer returned to pool via `free.deallocate(batch.buffer())`
    24→5. **Network client serialization
... (truncated)
68-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Kafka producer buffer pool race condition. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings

**Root Cause**: Messages appear on the wrong topic due to a race condition in buffer lifecycle management in `Sender.java`.

**The Race**:
1. Batch A's request is queued with the network client (`client.send()` at line 914)
2. Before serialization, Batch A expires and `failBatch()` is called
3. `failBatch()` immediately deallocates Batch A's buffer (line 835)
4. BufferPool reuses the buffer for new Batch B
5. Network client serializes Batch A's request but reads from the reused buffer containing Batch B's data
6. Corrupted request contains Batch B's topic/partition instead of Batch A's

**Why CRC Passes**: CRC only covers record key/value/headers, not the request header where the topic name is stored.

**The Fix**: 
Remove the premature deallocation from `failBatch()` (line 835 in Sender.java). Replace `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` with just `maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches()`. Let the buffer be deallocated later in `handleProduceResponse()` when it's safe, after serialization is complete.

The complete analysis with code diffs, execution flow diagrams, and detailed explanation has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

        

      

      

        Tool Calls (30)

result.unknownLeaderTopics)\\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\\n369: \\n370:             log.debug(\\\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched to send to\\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\\n385:                 iter.remove();\\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\\n387:             } else {\\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \\\"reset\\\" the node\\n389:                 // latency.\\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\\n391:             }\\n392:         }\\n393: \\n394:         // create produce requests\\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n402:             }\\n403:         }\\n404: \\n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\\n409: \\n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\\n414:             log.trace(\\\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\\\", expiredBatches.size());\\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\\n416:             String errorMessage = \\\"Expiring \\\" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \\\" record(s) for \\\" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\\n417:                 + \\\":\\\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \\\" ms has passed since batch creation\\\";\\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\\n422:             }\\n423:         }\\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\\n425: \\n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\\n435:             log.trace(\\\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\\\", result.readyNodes);\\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\\n441:         }\\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\\n443:         return pollTimeout;\\n444:     }\\n445: \\n446:     /**\\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\\n448:      */\\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n453:             return true;\\n454:         }\\n455: \\n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\\n460:         }\\n461: \\n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\\n464:             return false;\\n465: \\n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\\n468:         try {\\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\\n475:                     log.trace(\\\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\\\", targetNode);\\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n477:                     return true;\\n478:                 }\\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\\n480:                 log.trace(\\\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\\\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n482:                 return true;\\n483:             } else {\\n484:                 log.trace(\\\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\\\");\\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n487:                 return true;\\n488:             }\\n489: \\n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\\n492: \\n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\\n496:             log.debug(\\\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\\\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n500:             return true;\\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\\n502:             log.debug(\\\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \\\" +\\n503:                     \\\"to back off and retry.\\\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n506:             return true;\\n507:         }\\n508:     }\\n509: \\n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\\n513:         } else {\\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n517:         }\\n518: \\n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n520:     }\\n521: \\n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\\n524:             log.error(\\\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\\\", exception);\\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\\n526:         }\\n527:     }\\n528: \\n529:     /**\\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\\n531:      */\\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\\n536:         this.running = false;\\n537:         this.wakeup();\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     /**\\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\\n542:      */\\n543:     public void forceClose() {\\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\\n545:         initiateClose();\\n546:     }\\n547: \\n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\\n549:         return running;\\n550:     }\\n551: \\n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\\n572:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\\\",\\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, (response.wasDisconnected()) {\\n578:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\\\",\\n579:                 requestHeader,        for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\\n588:         } else {\\n589:             log.trace(\\\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\\\", response.destination(), correlationId);\\n590:             // if we have a response, // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\\n595:                 // This will be set by produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic                         new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618: {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\\n645:                 }\\n646:             }\\n647:         }\\n648:     }\\n649: \\n650:     /**\\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\\n787:                 } else {\\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\\n789:                 }\\n790:             }\\n791: \\n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\\n832:                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\\n833:                 }\\n834:             }\\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\\n859:     }\\n860: \\n861:     /**\\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\\n863:      */\\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\\n866:             return;\\n867: \\n868:         final {\n286:                 log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\n288:             }\n289:             log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\");\n290:             this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\n291:         }\n292:         try {\n293:             this.client.close();\n294:         } catch (Exception e) {\n295:             log.error(\"Failed to close network client\", e);\n296:         }\n297: \n298:         log.debug(\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\");\n299:     }\n300: \n301:     /**\n302:      * Run a single iteration of sending\n303:      *\n304:      */\n305:     void runOnce() {\n306:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n307:             try {\n308:                 transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\n309: \n310:                 RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\n311: \n312:                 // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\n313:                 if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\n314:                     if (lastError != null)\n315:                         maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\n316:                     client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n317:                     return;\n318:                 }\n319: \n320:                 if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\n321:                     return;\n322:                 }\n323: \n324:                 // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\n325:                 // request which will be sent below\n326:                 transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\n327: \n328:                 if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\n329:                     return;\n330:                 }\n331:             } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n332:                 // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\n333:                 log.trace(\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\", e);\n334:                 transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n335:             }\n336:         }\n337: \n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n339:         long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\n340:         client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\n341:     }\n342: \n343:     // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\n344:     // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\n345:     // instantiate the producer again.\n346:     private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\n347:         if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\n348:                         exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\n349:             transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\n350:             maybeAbortBatches(exception);\n351:             transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\n352:             return true;\n353:         }\n354:         return false;\n355:     }\n356: \n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n361: \n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n367:             for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\n369: \n370:             log.debug(\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\",\n371:                 result.unknownLeaderTopics);\n372:             this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n373:         }\n374: \n375:         // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n385:                 iter.remove();\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n387:             } else {\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n389:                 // latency.\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n391:             }\n392:         }\n393: \n394:         // create produce requests\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n402:             }\n403:         }\n404: \n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n409: \n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n414:             log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n416:             String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n417:                 + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n422:             }\n423:         }\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n425: \n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n435:             log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\n441:         }\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n443:         return pollTimeout;\n444:     }\n445: \n446:     /**\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n448:      */\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n453:             return true;\n454:         }\n455: \n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n460:         }\n461: \n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n464:             return false;\n465: \n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\n468:         try {\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\n475:                     log.trace(\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\", targetNode);\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n477:                     return true;\n478:                 }\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n480:                 log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n482:                 return true;\n483:             } else {\n484:                 log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n487:                 return true;\n488:             }\n489: \n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n492: \n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n496:             log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n500:             return true;\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\n502:             log.debug(\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \" +\n503:                     \"to back off and retry.\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n506:             return true;\n507:         }\n508:     }\n509: \n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\n513:         } else {\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n517:         }\n518: \n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n520:     }\n521: \n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\n524:             log.error(\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\", exception);\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\n526:         }\n527:     }\n528: \n529:     /**\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\n531:      */\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\n536:         this.running = false;\n537:         this.wakeup();\n538:     }\n539: \n540:     /**\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n542:      */\n543:     public void forceClose() {\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\n545:         initiateClose();\n546:     }\n547: \n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\n549:         return running;\n550:     }\n551: \n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is handled\n558:                 transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\n559:             }\n560:             return true;\n561:         }\n562:         return false;\n563:     }\n564: \n565:     /**\n566:      * Handle a produce response\n567:      */\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\n572:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\", response.destination())),\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\n578:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\",\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s\", response.destination())),\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n584:             log.warn(\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\",\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\n588:         } else {\n589:             log.trace(\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\", response.destination(), correlationId);\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\n604:                                 .stream()\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\n609: \n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n617: \n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\"Can't find batch created for topic id \" + r.topicId() +\n621:                                 \" topic name \" + r.name() + \" partition \" + p.index() + \" using \" + topicNames);\n622:                     }\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n624:                 }));\n625: \n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n630:                         .collect(\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\"For {} leader was updated.\", part)\n636:                         );\n637:                     }\n638:                 }\n639: \n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\n641:             } else {\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\n645:                 }\n646:             }\n647:         }\n648:     }\n649: \n650:     /**\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\n652:      *\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\n654:      * @param response The produce response\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n658:      */\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\n662: \n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\n667:             log.warn(\n668:                 \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n669:                 correlationId,\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n680:                 log.warn(\n681:                     \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n682:                     correlationId,\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\n691:                 //\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\n694:             } else {\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n699:             }\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n702:                     log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n703:                             \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\n705:                 } else {\n706:                     log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n707:                             \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n708:                 }\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n710:                     log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n715:                     }\n716:                 }\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n718:             }\n719:         } else {\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\n721:         }\n722: \n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n726:     }\n727: \n728:     /**\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n730:      * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n731:      */\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n734:                 \"\" : String.format(\". Error Message: %s\", response.errorMessage);\n735:         return String.format(\"%s%s\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\n736:     }\n737: \n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n742:     }\n743: \n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\n747:         }\n748: \n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n751:         }\n752:     }\n753: \n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\");\n762:         else\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\n764: \n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n767:         } else {\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\n779:                 } else {\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\n781:                 }\n782: \n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\n787:                 } else {\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\n789:                 }\n790:             }\n791: \n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\n795:                     return exception;\n796:                 } else {\n797: Final state, once set, is immutable. This function may be called\\n242:      * once or twice on a batch. It may be called twice if\\n243:      * 1. An inflight batch expires before a response from the broker is received. The batch's final\\n244:      * state is set to FAILED.   "content": "# Kafka Producer Buffer Pool Race Condition - Analysis and Fix\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java** \u2014 Entry point for bug investigation; contains `sendProducerData()` and `failBatch()` methods\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/ProducerBatch.java** \u2014 Batch lifecycle management; contains `records()` and `completeExceptionally()` methods\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/RecordAccumulator.java** \u2014 Buffer pool management; contains `deallocate()` method\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/BufferPool.java** \u2014 Buffer memory pooling (referenced via RecordAccumulator)\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Symptom observed in**: Produce requests silently corrupt topic/partition information; messages appear on wrong topic\n2. **Called from**: `Sender.sendProducerData()` (line 357) \u2014 orchestrates batch draining, expiration, and sending\n3. **Batch lifecycle**:\n   - Line 395: Batches drained from accumulator\n   - Line 396: Batches added to `inFlightBatches` tracking map\n   - Line 406-408: Expired batches detected from `inFlightBatches`\n   - Line 418: `failBatch()` called on expired batches\n   - Line 442: `sendProduceRequests()` sends non-expired batches to network client\n4. **Buffer deallocation path**:\n   - Line 835: `failBatch()` calls `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` (line 173)\n   - Line 173: Calls `accumulator.deallocate(batch)`\n   - RecordAccumulator line 1032: Buffer returned to pool via `free.deallocate(batch.buffer())`\n5. **Network client serialization**:\n   - Line 914: `client.send(clientRequest)` queues request for serialization\n   - Serialization happens later during `client.poll()` (line 340)\n   - Serialization reads from `batch.records()` buffer (line 874)\n\n## Root Cause\n\n- **File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java`\n- **Function**: `failBatch()` (line 817-837) and call chain from `sendProducerData()` (line 357)\n- **Line**: ~418 (expiration handling) and ~835 (deallocation)\n- **Exact issue**: Line 835 calls `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch)` unconditionally after marking batch as failed\n\n## Explanation of the Race Condition\n\n### The Bug\n\nWhen a `ProducerBatch` expires while its network request is still queued in the network client's send buffer, the following race occurs:\n\n1. **Iteration N of `sendProducerData()`**:\n   - Line 395: Batch A is drained and added to local `batches` map\n   - Line 396: Batch A is added to `inFlightBatches` (tracking map)\n   - Line 914: `client.send()` queues Batch A's produce request for later serialization\n\n2. **Before network client serialization** (within same or next iteration):\n   - Line 406-408: Batch A is found in `expiredInflightBatches` (delivery timeout reached)\n   - Line 418: `failBatch(Batch A)` is called\n   - Line 825: `batch.completeExceptionally()` returns true (first time setting final state to FAILED)\n   - Line 835: `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(Batch A)` is called\n   - Line 173: `accumulator.deallocate(Batch A)` is called\n   - RecordAccumulator line 1032: Batch A's ByteBuffer is returned to the `BufferPool`\n\n3. **BufferPool reuse** (concurrent with network serialization):\n   - BufferPool allocates Batch A's buffer to Batch B (new batch)\n   - Batch B writes records to the buffer\n\n4. **Network client serialization**:\n   - `client.poll()` (line 340) processes the queued request for Batch A\n   - Request serialization calls `batch.records()` (ProducerBatch line 481)\n   - `recordsBuilder.build()` returns MemoryRecords wrapping the original buffer\n   - **MemoryRecords does NOT copy data; it merely wraps the ByteBuffer reference**\n   - Serialization reads from the buffer, which now contains Batch B's data\n   - **Result**: Produce request header contains Batch B's topic/partition information instead of Batch A's\n\n### Why This Corrupts the Topic Name\n\nThe produce request format has two parts:\n1. **Header** (contains topic name, partition, etc.) \u2014 part of ProduceRequest structure\n2. **Records payload** \u2014 MemoryRecords wrapping the batch's ByteBuffer\n\nThe header is serialized from the batch's metadata AFTER the buffer has been deallocated and reused. When the buffer is reused, the topic name in the header becomes corrupted with data from the reused buffer.\n\n### Why CRC Validation Passes\n\nThe CRC checksum (ProduceResponse) covers only:\n- Key/value data\n- Headers\n- **NOT** the topic name (which is in the request header, not the record batch)\n\nTherefore, corrupted topic names bypass CRC validation.\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\nThe root cause is that `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` is called in `failBatch()` while the batch's request may still be queued in the network client.\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\n**Do NOT deallocate batches in the `failBatch()` path. Let them be deallocated through the normal response path in `handleProduceResponse()` or through explicit cleanup on disconnect.**\n\n### Code Changes\n\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java`\n\n#### Change 1: Remove premature deallocation in failBatch()\n\n```diff\n--- a/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java\n+++ b/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java\n@@ -828,13 +828,22 @@ public class Sender implements Runnable {\n      * we need to reset the producer id here.\n      */\n     private void failBatch(\n         ProducerBatch batch,\n         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\n         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n     ) {\n         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n\n         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\n             if (transactionManager != null) {\n                 try {\n                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\n                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\n                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n                 } catch (Exception e) {\n                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\n                 }\n             }\n-            maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n+            // Note: We do NOT deallocate the batch here, even though its final state is now set to FAILED.\n+            // The batch may still have an active request queued in the network client's send buffer.\n+            // Deallocating the buffer here would cause the buffer to be returned to the pool and potentially\n+            // reused by another batch while the network client is still serializing this batch's request.\n+            // This would corrupt the serialized request data (topic name, partition, etc).\n+            // Instead, we only remove the batch from inFlightBatches tracking. The buffer will be deallocated\n+            // when the response is eventually received (or the connection times out/disconnects) in handleProduceResponse().\n+            maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n         }\n     }\n```\n\n#### Change 2: Handle deallocation of failed batches that complete through handleProduceResponse()\n\nThe existing code in `handleProduceResponse()` already handles deallocation properly:\n- Line 750 in `completeBatch()`: `if (batch.complete(...)) { maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch); }`\n\nThis code attempts to set the batch's final state to SUCCEEDED. If the batch was already marked FAILED, this will fail gracefully (ProducerBatch.done line 277-286 handles the FAILED -> SUCCEEDED transition by logging and ignoring). The batch will remain in `inFlightBatches` until:\n\n1. A response from broker arrives and is processed in `handleProduceResponse()`\n2. Network disconnect is detected (handled in same method at line 577-582)\n3. Request timeout occurs (handled at line 571-576)\n\nIn all these cases, `completeBatch()` is called which will deallocate the batch at line 750 via `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()`.\n\n#### Change 3: Add defensive guard for batches already deallocated\n\nTo handle any edge cases where a batch might be processed twice, add safety check in `deallocate()`:\n\n```diff\n--- a/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/RecordAccumulator.java\n+++ b/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/RecordAccumulator.java\n@@ -1027,8 +1027,14 @@ public class RecordAccumulator {\n      */\n     public void deallocate(ProducerBatch batch) {\n         incomplete.remove(batch);\n         // Only deallocate the batch if it is not a split batch because split batch are allocated outside the\n         // buffer pool.\n         if (!batch.isSplitBatch())\n-            free.deallocate(batch.buffer(), batch.initialCapacity());\n+            // Only deallocate if the batch still has its buffer. In rare cases, the batch might be\n+            // processed multiple times (e.g., marked failed via timeout, then receives response from broker).\n+            // Once deallocated, the buffer reference becomes invalid.\n+            if (batch.buffer() != null) {\n+                free.deallocate(batch.buffer(), batch.initialCapacity());\n+            }\n     }\n```\n\n## Analysis: Execution Flow Demonstrating the Bug\n\n### Normal (non-buggy) case:\n1. Batch drained at T1, request queued at T2, serialized at T3, response received at T4, deallocated at T4\n2. Buffer stays allocated while network client owns the request\n\n### Buggy case (what we fixed):\n1. Batch drained at T1\n2. Request queued at T2\n3. **Batch expires and marked FAILED at T2.5**\n4. **Buffer deallocated and returned to pool at T2.7**\n5. **New batch B allocated and reuses buffer at T2.8**\n6. Network client serializes request for batch A at T3\n7. **Corruption: Request has batch B's data in the buffer**\n8. Corrupted request sent to broker at T4\n9. Messages appear on wrong topic\n\n### Fixed case:\n1. Batch drained at T1\n2. Request queued at T2\n3. Batch expires and marked FAILED at T2.5\n4. **Buffer NOT deallocated** (fix prevents this)\n5. Network client serializes request for batch A at T3\n6. **Request has correct data from batch A's buffer**\n7. Response received at T4\n8. Batch deallocated at T4 (in handleProduceResponse)\n9. Buffer can now be reused safely\n\n## Summary\n\nThe race condition occurs because `failBatch()` deallocates a batch's buffer before the network client finishes serializing its request. By moving the deallocation to the `handleProduceResponse()` path (which is guaranteed to execute after serialization), we ensure the buffer remains valid throughout the entire request lifecycle.\n",
